de l’enfleure des piez	of the unveiling of the limbs
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the limbs are uncovered to the wet one, and they are plain like citron, it is necessary that you cauterize on the back of it between the auricular and the anus; and gently place your hand with the cautery without turning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too much in front, otherwise the awl will break, and follow this form for the cauterization:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	Afterwards, make two cauterizations on each leg at the tip of the nail; and let the cauterizations be long enough to curve, one in front of the genital area and the other behind, along the leg; and leave the cauterizations to cure for a long time before removing them; after the cure of the other cures that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of the menstruation
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	When the belly comes from cold and moisture, as the digestive and absorptive virtues in the stomach and intestines are swollen and inflamed, and cannot be cured by usual means; and you see the patient suffering greatly and with weak constitution, if you make a large cauterization on the stomach according to what has been spoken of before or on the small intestine, around the cauterization; and then make four small cauterizations subtle at all the clavicle subtle, and two cauterizations on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see the moisture abundant and the patient suffering, then perform the cautery on the point, and the cautery on each side, and the cauterization on the stomach of the great wound, because the cure is beneficial when it has good aid.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the cure of epistaxis (nosebleeds)
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	When the epistaxis is either fundamental, or one or more, and are old and large humors cold and moist corrupted, and are treated as we have said in divisions, and if not profitable, if you make cauterizations: III on the spine of the back, which is entirely deflated and flattened in triangulation, and the cauterization on the bowel II doses; and if you think that his stomach is cooled, and the meat is not cooked, and you see the face swelling, then the face on the greatest cauterization on the stomach, as it is said before, and the other on the liver, and the other on the gallbladder at all the cauterizations closed; and leave the cauterization over long.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After curing the wound as much as it is healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the charnosite which is called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you apply thecautery, if it seems to be the rasor, and then place it completely on the affected area of the althelul; and leave as much of your hand as the cauteries will reach at the birth of the vein, without cutting; do this once or twice, and if it does not help, cauterize another one as we have said; after the cure of wounds as much as they are healthy; and if you cauterize with a large cautery on the alchatim, it will give more help.
de plaie mal curee	Of a wound improperly treated
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure cutting or opening, which we will tell you in his case, if a serious illness comes that cannot be healed by cauterization alone.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When there is no fistula, and it is awake and gushing sour milk and rotten moisture, if you provide enough of a tent, and keep hold of the whole tent as much as it has to.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After scraping the cauterization that appears to be a rasping tool, and pulling it out of the fistula according to the quantity that enters, and resumes the cauterization as much as the corners are pricked and corrupted; and you should wear leather gloves on the hands that are wet, and large wounds.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	1. If the fistula wishes to go into the course of the vein and the intestine, if you were to do this, and only make it as in the gallbladder, and think that it is not a human one; then cure the gallbladder as much as it is healthy, and if the fistula is removed, and the materials are long bones, then know that the gallbladder is completely healthy; and if the materials are not long bones, know that the gallbladder is in its place, and the bones are corrupted at the root; and then, as one of these that we will say in his gallbladder.
de la maladie des reins	2. of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When pain in the head comes on suddenly, and with large ventritis, and no woman is at hand, then it is necessary that you first cauterize the wounds on both sides of the head using the cautery we have mentioned before; and if we cauterize in a line, there will be three cauterizations in line, and they will provide more aid.
de la vessie	of the uterus
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the uterus is large and weak in head and neck, if the patient retains urine, then first cauterize the part around the vagina on the uterus, where the hair grows, both on the right and left sides, and make each cauterization as long as one of our fingers; and then cauterize the back of the vagina, or II if you want to do so; and so make the cauterizations according to the form mentioned before.
de la marris	Of the married woman
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the wife is cold and moist, and does not allow any for conception, and the flow is corrupted and delayed; and when they come, if they feel great pain: therefore it is necessary to make three cauteries along the belly, as we have said or about the cauterization of the vesicle, and then cauterize the back; and if the cauterization is by nail, as we have said.
de la hainche	of the shoulder
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When the viscous moisture descends to the shoulder socket, and for this reason if it does not move from its place, and the sign is that the shoulder is longer than the other when measured together; and it is found that the leu departments are very wide, if it comes that you cauterize the patient on the shoulder socket at the cautery like a circle, and sew before the leu on the shoulder so that the shoulder turns the circle; and if it is the cauterization like those we have done on the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if this cauterization is not present, make three large olive-wood cauterizations, and they should be as sharp as the thorns; and the cure will be made when it is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	for the pain of the hernia
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes in the hernia bag, and it is cold and moist, and the patient is cured as we have said in the division, and the cure does not work, and the disease is old: then it is necessary to purge the patient of large humors from bitter pills or other bone-like pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After the cauterization; and the way to cauterize is according to two ways: it is known to assemble burning medicines, and to cauterize with fire.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	1. If the fire cautery is done according to methods, then some are like this: you cauterize on the hair root of the beard III cauterize triangularly according to this form, and make good depth and large size, and leave between each cauterization a space of an inch, and it is olive oil; never cauterize on the same spot of the beard more than four times according to this form.
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	2. And if you see, if the cauterization is done at the circle we mentioned in the dislocation of the beard; but do it in such a way that the circles contain the entire beard, and all its corners are even.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way it is done in sciatica, when the pain holds in the hip and does not reach the thigh or knee.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And when the pain comes to the thigh and knee, if the patient feels it in the hip and thigh or knee, then cauterize there as the malaide says that the pain is held, and cut out four pieces of flesh, on the side part least; and whether it is the cauterizing cautery or the sharp edge of the knife, if the malaide feels that the pain spreads to two points or close to it, then cauterize at that point which is called "points".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	When the pain is not relieved, make it a cauterization; and if the pain is towards the thigh, then cauterize with the cutaneous or circular cauterization, and take good care of all your cauterizations that you do not burn too much the cauterization but the nerves and the large arteries, and do not cause more harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	I have also seen cases where they cauterized on the ankle, and they burned so much that the entire leg became inflamed, and the foot as well, and it was noticed and corrupted all the toes.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a solution of the stomach, where he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two parts together, make a fire cautery on both, according to this method.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And the patient says in the fire cautery of the thigh, according to this method, make such a metal and it should be at the head as big as some anvil dough, or a smaller one, and it should be intertwined and it should be of the same size as the piece of an iron nail; and the intertwining parts should be over two parts, and they should also be like noses, and it should have a good handle; and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	1. And let it be shaved as long as it is red and greasy, then place it on the handle of the male shaving brush, and make it curve once around the cauterization; and then apply a plaster, and leave the wound open for three days; and then apply ointment after the cure is complete, as it becomes healthy.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	1. Albucasim says that we use little of this cauterant due to its fear, and if we use it little, then all this is cauterizing ointment that can be endured, and either he will wipe it off.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The first sentence to translate is: "The medicinal cauterization if you have an instrument to cross the cheek at the edge of the door, and it is either of iron or of steel a certain distance, and in the upper part it has two of us, and between each of them the quantity of growth of a toe; and they overgrow and pierce, and they join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After putting the iron of the broom on the patient's shoulder, gripping your hand tightly around the broom handle; after applying heat between the two circles of the heated awl that is heated in the fire, and leaves it for an hour, suffering from the patient's chill and artery pain.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	For true mordication is like fire; when the mordication has passed, ease your hand with the instrument and raise the awl gently, leaving it for three hours, and then put on bandages as much as necessary to cover the wound, and leave them on until the dressing becomes saturated; and this will be helpful after the care of wounds as soon as they are healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And if the pain spreads to the thigh or leg, make an instrument that traces according to what you have done in the hair; and this is the way of the hot tool, and I have written or described the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Add alkaline and live charcoal, as much of one as of the other, and mix them together, and put them in the new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	Or if there is a small hole that the point of a razor can go through and cut; and then put some of this powder into another pot well filled, and add alkaline and charcoal and soft ash until you have two parts of the powder you will have well mixed in your hand; and leave it until it comes down with water or clay, then take all of this powder, and mix it with charcoal and alkaline as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	When it is boiling and the patient is in a state of mind and under the influence of medicines and cauterizations of other parts, she makes autumn work like fire, and if other medicines are used that are well cauterized on the thigh, such as honey and anacardium and chalz with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	Galiens also tells us of a cure where some were cured of the pain in the thigh and sciatica, and he says that no other cure is needed, and that it was cured once for every time this cure was made, and he was bathed as he instructed afterward.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And then, in a certain way, you should shave the affected area with fresh and dry hair, and grease it with a little grease, and put it on the shoulder, thigh, and leg where the pain is, and tie it; and leave it for three hours, according to the amount that the patient no longer feels the discomfort.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then, I put it in a bath as long as the chest is raised, and I let it enter the fire, and the pain will all leave and be healthy.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	I advise that no one should use such a burning medicine, unless it is after the evacuation of blood.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And Dyascorides says that when the sciatic nerve is cauterized with the horn of a goat, if it helps pain; and it must be made in a certain way.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take the fat and melt it with oil, and put it in the socket which is between the little finger and the other which is called the ham.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	After drying the goat horn, and burning it until it is charred, and then putting it on the wool, and leaving it as long as it is red; and do it again and continue doing it as much as you think it will reach the hip bone, and that the pain is subsided; and this way of cauterization is called "cauterization with goat horn".
de la dolor dou dos	Of the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether by touching or percussion or from too great an evacuation, or from the appearance of expanded cold matter, none of these appearances is worth cauterization, rather it is for the one that comes from the infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary after the patient has been made clean by removing pus or other appearances, to cut on the back of the shoulder where the pain remains, three lines are marked with a scalpel, and in each line V cauterization or more according to the skill and quantity that the patient can bear; and it should be done according to the cautery called "points"; and if you see, make III cauterizations or IIII on the scalpel handle according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	This malady often affects many children, and the signs of its onset are seen when they tighten their legs as they grow, and fear; and you see the spines on their backs and the appearance that comes from the other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and it is cured, if it is cauterized at the cauterization point according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If the cauterization turns purple on every part of the spine equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, if cauterization is done along the spine at the cauterization point pricking II or III lines, and these points are close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After treating the wound as much as it is healthy according to what we have said, and make sure that you do not perform a fire cautery on the bone that is in the spine of the nose.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When pain in the joints comes from moisture that is expanded to each member of the body, and when pain comes with swelling, which they call "gout" properly, and when it is cold cause and medicines do not cure it, then it is cured by cauterization in this way: make the gout on the outside of the joint, and it should be olive oil according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if you intend to prick at the face of a child, then cauterize all of it as claimed in the "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if the pain comes to the groin and other joints, and this happens many times, then cauterize each groin three times or four times on the whole olive-wood cauterization tool; and if you have skill for more, but do not hold your hand as long as the pain allows.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pain descends to the groin and the back, apply the cauterization we have mentioned in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	If the pain remains in the hand, make points on the second line of the frost; and if there is no more pain, make points on each joint and on the hair of the hand; and if the pain comes from the wrists or shoulders, cauterize each part, and govern the patient's behavior with medicine.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you make the patient behave and purge the fever, they will be cured by God.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rupture of the uterus
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	If the rupture comes in waves, and the children descend quickly and suddenly, so that when you see it being cured, it does not return to its place; and if he uses things that soften the belly, so that the child descends from his belly; then make him lie on his back between your hands, and command that he lick his anus as much as he can, and tie it with strings to your two fingers, and sew it around the bone of the lower part of the abdomen, and make a sign that it is like half of a circle around the two curves of the belly; then wash the cauterization with the following form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	As long as it is white and it glistens.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then bend the thighs at the knee; and the surgeon should mark his hand to ensure they do not return; and well exercise the thighs on the patient, and put a bandage on each thigh, and the other on the knee that he has marked on the thighs; then place the cautery at the sign of all the hand, and hold it right and as far as you can reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, continue again until you touch the bone; and be gentle so that the blood does not flow when you make the cautery; that you do not burn it; and that by this the surgeon does not die, or another.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And you should know that when you do not reach the bone in the cauterization, your efforts are in vain.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it is necessary that the cauterization of children be done subtly according to the size of the bone, and the same for grown people; after three days, cure the wound of the needle as much as the burn is healed; after the cure of other ointments as long as they are healthy, and grease his nails forty days on his back as long as the wound is well sore; and it is necessary that his hair be left long and untrimmed, so that the dung does not stick when he goes to the chamber.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	After forty days, when he wishes to rise, he will find a well-made cut on his arm, and every four days thereafter; and he should rest, so that he works quickly and does not have too much overflow of drinking and eating, and does not have too high fever; and when he teaches this lesson, it is completely healthy.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say this after the cauterization in his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the stomach
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When ruptures occur in other stomachs and are known, and you see that they do not increase, he should be cauterized according to the quantity, and it should be done in the third form; after the treatment according to what we have said; and no of the ancients have said that it should be cauterized at the cautery with three angles according to this form.
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	But the first sign of the shoulder is to make a line for the widest part of the fracture, and another one, and hold your hand on all the cauterization clamps.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	However, the first cauterizations are more gentle and less painful.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	and no pain in any part of the body.
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes from any part of the body, whether it is from chilling or wounding, and this pain lasts for a long time, and the cure with medicine does not help, then it is necessary to cauterize at the cauterization point called "points", and to make the cauterization according to the length of the affected member, the thinness and strength of the flesh, the location of the torsions and the pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If the first cauterization is healthy, it's well; but if not, restart another cauterization on the same part, because it is customary that one must die in the member that is proximate, since it is necessary to do the cauterizations as long as the malady remains.
de meselerie	of medicine
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The remedies are never helped by cauterization once, and at the same time, the disease that comes from the putrefaction of flesh and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	Can you see the cauterization, take care if the disease is at the beginning, and cure it according to what we have said in the division, and do not hesitate if the corruption does not corrupt all the malady, therefore I make the cauterization on the head: I cut off the head, and the other towards the front at the end of the thighs; and they touch the horns, and the heels touch the hock; and it lasts as much as your hand that the cauterization sticks to the bone, and as much as the effusions come out so that the vapors of the large humors can come out; and I cauterize on the anus according to what is before.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	1. If the scar is scattered everywhere; it is clearly evident if you cauterize the wound with these cauterizing methods that we have mentioned or chief, and the cauterization is in one place, and the cauterizations on the spine of the neck, and on the spine of the back, and on the knee and the other elbow, and the shoulders, and the wrists, and the tendons of the ankles, and all the joints of the hands and feet, and the sockets of the hands; and you will find nerves that are located below the skin, which you must not burn, and never cauterize on the bone of the fingertips, or the other bone of the stomach, or the other bone of the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	When more you burn, the more help it gives, and benefits the patient; and advise that the patient does not feel pain at the burn if the physician does not, because the heart is already corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	It is necessary that the burn be large and small according to the members and joints, according to what you will find in the manner of iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After curing the wound with flour several times with honey and other remedies until it is healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the wound is healed and treated with medicines and oils and plasters, and it is not healthy, then the burn is made on the member according to the size and smallness of the member; and let the burn be entered into the end of the small joint; then the treatment of ointments as long as it is healthy.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	For no time is it done that the cautery is made on the hand, arm, and back, at the end of the bone that holds the member, and otherwise if it is forced; and none enters if they are not known of the members and the movements of the bones in the body.
de albaras	of bars
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the disease called "albaras" is awakened, and the art of medicine does not help, then the cautery is made with a cautery piece, according to the quantity of the ointment, until the blenching is forced and the color becomes pale; then the care of flour and lentils with rose oil and plantain leaves, and saffron and almond oil, for each part; and all are assembled, and tied with a piece of cloth, and applied to the body as much as it is needed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of syphilis by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When the gumma appears at the beginning, and you see it stop, if you cauterize it with a fire cautery that seems to form a circle, all around the circumference of the gumma.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And the old doctors said that cauterization is also done in the environment of the gumma; and I think it is not very good, because I doubt that it will not become ulcerated and corrupted, and I have always wanted to see this happen once; and the most correct thing is that it is cauterized around, with a fire cautery called "circular," as we have said in our mouths about cauterization.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	The first sentence to translate is "de l'enfleure qui ne puet meurer". The translation of this line is "from
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	If someone has a disease called "adubelati", and it delays in dying either due to excessive treatment or because the patient is too old (too many years) and lacks blood, or for other reasons, and you see it hurting: then, the cauterization is performed by making small cuts with the cautery; afterwards, it is left alone.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will die in dying.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it hastening to die, if the cautery is too hot, then its form is like this:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	When you have a disease called "adubelati", keep your hand in the environment of that disease as long as the cauterization has perceived the heat, and such cauterization that the patient feels it in a way that the course of the sweat is altered slightly.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment when it is completely cured.
li cure dou feu par fer	the cure by fire with iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another way of disease is called "corrodens", and it is nothing but a mangle of the limb, because it mangles the limbs as well as the dry sticks.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this disease in the leg that can suffer cauterization together with fire, then sharpen the cauterizations clavile as small and large as it can go according to the leg or the disease; after cauterizing all parts as much as you can, remove all of it, that nothing remains of it, which is corrupted, that everything that is corrupted is not osteit.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Then let it remain for three days, and put on the burned parts with oil, suffering burns with fat as long as the burned parts are not healed and the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the cure of burns generated by fire.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if after three days no healthy burns are born, it is good; and if not, continue the cauterization on the parts that need it the most.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	And this disease has never been cured by medical treatment in the place of fire cauterization; but all cauterization with fire is greater help, and I have already said that the cure of the ague by medical treatment is in the division: take what you have in your possession.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	Of the porers who come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times it has happened that the feet were infected with a disease called "closed" according to our understanding, and it is a large thing that must be treated to ease the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the treatment of this disease is in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	It is to know that the treatment of this disease is either by fire cauterization or hot water cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Fire cauterization is when you heat the foot with fire and use hot water as a cauterizing agent, which is like a needle of copper made as large as it can hold the nail of all parts, and has sharp margins; after that, you put everything around the nail and turn your hand totally around the nail as much as it comes to the end of the nail; then it leaves for three days until it begins to run milk; then I make a poultice of well-cooked herbs with milk, and leave the poultice on all night, and the nails will be pulled out of their roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then, treat the wound with ointment as soon as it is clean.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	And if the wound becomes infected many times, and in the hands and fingers, then it is necessary that you have a fire cautery; and it is done in this way: take a piece of iron or steel, or a feather, and insert it into the nail and the horn, as to make warts disappear; then put the iron on so that it burns everything around, then put a little hot water, and hold your hand well, and press your hand as you turn until the margin of the iron reaches the root of the nail, and it will find the hot water nicely fitted at the root; then suffer the pain of the hot water for a while; then leave it alone, and it will all fall off at all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	You then make another cut, as long as you are careful with all these that are in the course, and treat the wounds that have been pierced by the arrow.
li cure dou trembler	and do not tremble.
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee; et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	If any tremble from cold or fever, or other cause, then it is necessary that you make four cauteries or four on the spine, one cauterization between each spine; and one at the stomach with olive oil cautery; if this stops the trembling, and helps to recover from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of pustules that have been opened.
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	There is no occasion for the appearance of abscesses or pustules, which come from large corrupt materials.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	If it is necessary to cauterize at the first appearance of the pustule, a subtle cauterization with mirth wood, or if the point is held in the fire, or with the root of Aristolochia long, or with the lenticular cauterization.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And never is cauterization done at the beginning when they appear, according to this manner, and they do not grow new branches in front, but are disturbed by the superfluity that comes, and are healthy; but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	Many times there are great hemorrhages of blood from the artery that is cut at the wound that comes to the perineum, or at the incision of the abscess, or at the fire cautery of the limb, and similar things; and it is a very sad thing to have to open.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And if there is none, then when you have to put your finger index on the vein wound, and hold it as tightly as possible until it becomes calm and your finger is no longer painful; then heat the olive oil cauteries more often smaller and larger until they are all red; then I, or according to the size of the wound and the strength of the limb and the artery that is cut, put the cautery on this wound or where you hold your finger, and hold the cautery as tightly as possible until it becomes painless.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	If the fire cautery has stopped burning when you loosen your child's vein, and it is cold, then quickly take another one that is hot.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And continue to do this until it is stretched; and watch that you do not burn the nerve that is sensitive, and that no other harm comes to the patient; and be careful when the artery is not extended, that it does not become worse immediately when the artery becomes large, if it is not by one of the four methods we have mentioned: either by cauterization or extraction, or by tightening with thread, or by medicines applied which can cause inflammation; and be careful and extract.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever will tightly tie the knots of threads or to hang things on, or other similar things, should not profit from it if it is not possible.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if there is none, and there is no medicine present, then he should put his index finger on the wound of the vein as we have said, and firmly press until it is painful in the wound and the vein; and he should not move, but his finger should be often cold, so that it does not freeze and becomes numb and painful; and make sure to use those that are skilled in cauterization and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here comes the first sentence to translate:
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	For the first chapter of medicine, we have told you about all diseases that require fire cauterization or burning medicine, and their causes, effects, and forms of cauterization; and I have taken the lead in this chapter, and I will go to this chapter by my own way because it is lighter to come here.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	However, before I begin this, it is necessary that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first cauterizations, and for this reason there is greater caution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses; ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	I advise you not to attempt foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For there are many ways of people coming for treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice; et de ces doit on avoir paor.	If they come from those who have been so severely affected by their illness that they die easily due to the treatment they receive for their disease, and because of this we must fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit: «atendez, je sui garis»; et li maladie est despitouse.	And there are those who understand your sense and say: "Wait, I am almost dead"; and the disease is hopeless.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los; et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie; et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	It is only necessary that you allow those who come to you to have this manner, but put more trust in your honor than in your covetousness, and do not fear too much but rather wisely of what you are certain, and what you could have taken or lost; and use prognosis and indication in the cures of your patients for the conversion of health; and this will help to achieve this good reputation, glory, and memory.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Three-fingered, our Lords give you understanding and straightness, and if you will strive for the holy inspiration of its hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	I have commanded this chapter to you in indicating by chapters, according as it is before or after cauteries, which I have indicated for the chief joints, because you will find it more easily what you will have to do.
dou chief plein d’aigue	A full-grown chief with inflammation
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant; et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	Sicknesses that this disease comes from time to time in children's wombs, and when it is drawn too strongly from the child's head; and never has it come from a cured cause that it is not.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors; et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	The patient will always suffer from this disease only in children, and in all those I have seen, death follows; therefore, it seems to me that I should briefly mention the treatment in some cases.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir; et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os; et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large; et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre; et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	I have seen a child with acute sore throat, and the mother engrossed it every day until she could no longer bear it; she thought this moisture was the cause of death, and this moisture is found between the knee and the thigh, between the bone and the knee; if the ovary is like this, and the moisture is between the bone and the knee, and the abscesses are small, then you should give the child a large pus pouch; and so long as the moisture continues, the form of the spatulum will be like this.
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more intense, and the abscess is larger, then I will make incisions in this manner:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut: si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	If the moisture has reached the bone, and you see the edges of the chest overstretched in each part, and the wound gushes out when you press with your hand on the dedens, and this has not been noticed before: then it may be necessary to cut the chest III times according to this method:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, remove all the moisture.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor; puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	After removing the dressings and powders, and applying wine and oil, and leaving it for five days; then remove the bandage, and cure the wound with poultices and ointments, and leave the chest evenly bandaged, and then apply dry, moisture-free meat to the scar as much as possible until the member is comfortable and healthy.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue; car aucune fois est elle devant; aucune fois derrier; aucune fois en destre; et aucune fois en senestre.	And another way of incision is to look at or open the aperture of the abscess, and the assembled angle; for it is never in front; never on the back; never in the side; and never in the front.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir; et warde que tu ne coper l’artere; et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	Therefore, measure the size of the abscess opening and the angle of the wedge, and they are made according to what you can afford; and do not cut the artery; and come forward with blood, if the patient dies from loss of blood and evacuation of moisture.
de reume	of remedy
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When a disease called "catarrh" occurs in the ears or throat, and the disease is ancient, and the cure by medicine does not help much, therefore it is cured with cauterization if one cuts off the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief; aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel; puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues; puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	1. It is therefore necessary, can you see the eyes, that the patient makes a cut on his head; afterwards, rub the leg with a rough cloth as much as the arteries are visible, then tighten the cloth around the neck all around; then look if the wound bleeds, and the blood from both sides is after the ears, and few are replenished; then sign the legs are swelling, then cover one and the other with a damp sponge of II parts, as much as the size comes to the bone, and that is by the wide head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	2. And if you see, soak the sponge in water and cover the artery with it, cutting as much as II does to the bone, and that is by the wide head.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	When the vein is cut, if the blood continues to flow unceasingly.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os; et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere; puis regarde la plaie: s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	And if the artery does not open upon feeling, then measure the amount of blood that escapes for three minutes, and then apply a bandage and press hard against the bone; and if it is necessary to pour out six cups of blood, and perhaps more or less depending on what the patient can bear, and the replenishment of the artery, then look at the wound: if it remains above the bone without causing pain, and the cut that was made does not bleed, then tighten the wound and leave it until it is healed.
de emigrainne	From migration
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When the head migrates, and becomes puffy, with moisture from tears and saliva in the temples, and sometimes other strange things, it is treated with medicines of various kinds, but nothing helps, if we burn the arteries of the temples and cauterize, as we have experienced.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit; et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement; puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	And the manner of extracting them if the patient has hair on his temples, and understands the artery that opens in the temple, because it opens well by its beating, and is quickly repaired in most men who are too impatient; and when it is repaired, if he tightens his collar with his hands, then rub the inside of his neck with a rough cloth, and rinse the inside of his neck with hot water until the artery opens clearly; then take the spatula of that form:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie; et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	Then lightly burn the soft leather until you feel the artery, then tear it up high as possible, and cut off as many strips as there are in each part; and if the artery is subtle, and the tip turns towards the nail, then the piece of that part follows according to the number of the II chiés.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not cut, then it will not be broken at all.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III; et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc; puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez; et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And cut out as much blood as sixth parts of a gallon, and if the artery is large, then it will be tied with two strong silk threads of the same size as the wound, so that nothing comes before the solid of the wound, and comes off with the sanguine; then cut off the superfluity that is between the sixth parts of the limbs in that hour, and then, if you see, if the cauterization is done with hot fire as much as the bone until the chiés are burned; and this is the most difficult work, if the patient has no fever and is of warm complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors: por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	For the fire cautery is help to finally end the moisture: for it is of greater aid to the moisture.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites; et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez; et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez; et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient; et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	For the extraction of arteries is required when they are filled with much soft cloth and placed in well-made tents; and if you loosen them, whether you treat them with dry medicines that make them turn red and swell, or with tents as long as it is safe; and if there is no cut to the artery as you wish, then use the lee of vitrol and hold it in your hand that it may not be stained; and if you do not have this present, then put some of the lee of your own body as much as it may freeze, and wet it with cold water so that it may never freeze again, and draw it as it is necessary; and what is most difficult and lightest in the extraction of arteries is that you cauterize the vein of this cautery trenching from the second part, but the trenching should be well spaced to last longer with less pain.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the wound is too deep, it holds less blood.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus; et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And it must have between two and three pieces of spice, and then when you have filled the two holes with spice, put your fire on as hot as it can reach the bone, and cover the wound with the two pieces; and they should be separated by the two points because it is not always the case that this cauterization works in everything; and this is the form of cauterization:
des larmes	of tears.
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis; et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	When the tears of the eyes descend down the veins that are located in the forehead, and it does not profit much from medicine, and you see the face of the patient writhing, and you hear the front ambulation as if it were a cataclysm; and they are thin and moist so that the paper of the eyes look cut, and the papers are shredded by the heat of the tears, if it has to do with this cure.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front; et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres; et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins; et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	1. And they called the old "bruised cure," and that is when you treat the patient who has this disease with his hair or front, then make three incisions on the front according to the length of the front; and one of the incisions is like the other two at the back, advancing the knife without touching the neck, and the others are the costals through the papers, and keep away from the incision of the arteries that are the costals through the papers; and separate your hand from the continuation of the mandibles, and each wound is the quantity of three to the traverse joints; and you have appeared a piece of sponge and moisten the cloth with his sweat coming out of the pain, then cut the spatule of the two parts that is the form:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision; et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	1. "From the incision that is made in the temple until the second incision; and scarps all the flesh that is between the two fences up to the entire bone that is seen on the bone, then makes another cut at the other side of the first second incision, and then extracts this splinter.

"If blood is drawn in the first fence with the instrument called 'cultivator', and it is very sharp on one side but very blunt on the other side, do not make it too sharp, and this is the shape:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	3. "And make the costal cut towards the arm and the costal bone, and the costal blade towards the bone, and the blood as much as it reaches to the second incision.

And cut all the veins that hang down as much as the incision is continued until it opens a little, and then another part of the bone is cut until it is divided; and then draw out the blood evenly, and express the leeway for the blood taken; then put in each fence a small piece of soft cotton, and put over it fluffed linen cloths soaked in wine and oil, and ointment, and keep them from coming; and when the limb is loose, and apply large amounts of tincture of wormwood with rose oil, and other ointments that are used to heal wounds, as long as it is healthy.
dou reume des eulz	It seems like there might be a missing word or a typo in the sentence you
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees; et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue; adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	When there is no familiar cautery, and you see the hairs thinning and breaking, and the papers burning; and the hair falling out, and the skin becoming inflamed, and the wound bleeding; therefore, be careful with these accidents, as those materials and this cautery only come from many veins, and the cure that is in it, if it is this.

And begin the incision from the left temple to the right temple, and make it cut through the bone; and pull your hand away from the temples that move in the cheek; and when the bone is exposed, take all the blood that comes out and place it on a sponge, then put cotton between the two lips of the incision, and wrap it with linen; then cover the wound with dampened cloth and oil, and keep your fingers from getting cold; when it is healed, if it comes to the point where it starts to scab over, then the care of things that are exfoliating, which cause the skin to peel, will be necessary.
